[ 1 ] 
JUDICIAL NOTIFICATION
UNCLAIMED DEPOSITS IN THE CITY CIVIL COURT, CHENNAI - 104
(Dis. No. 12921/LS)
No. VI(1)/7/2023
Notice is hereby given that the undermentioned items of deposits above Rs.5/- in the 
City Civil Court Chennai for the years 2013-2014 Under Deposit Accounts were kept as unclaimed 
for more than 4 years that unless the parties entitled to them appear and claim them on or before 
31st January 2023, those items of deposits will be lapsed and credited to Government Account 
under Rule 54 of Section (1) and under Rule 119(d)(i) of section II of Civil Rule of Practice and 
Circular Orders Volume II.
